###  Tiikki₁

This rare proper noun overlaps more common *Tiikki* (FIXME)
* UPOS:  PROPN
* in KOTUS dictionary under:  5
* Origin:  finer
* Possible NER class:  GEO
* Blacklisted:  PROPN-BLOCKING
